# [Kubernetes] Add NoScheduleNoTraffic Taint Effect

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.30.0 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/kubernetes--v1.30.0 (mirror of kubernetes/kubernetes)  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#2-kubernetes-noschedulenotraffic-taint-effect)

## Description

Implement a new Node taint effect called `NoScheduleNoTraffic` that:
1. **Prevents new pods from being scheduled** (like `NoSchedule`)
2. **Removes the node from Service EndpointSlices** (affects traffic routing)
3. **Does NOT evict existing pods** (unlike `NoExecute`)

This is a distinct effect from existing `NoSchedule` (which doesn't affect traffic) and `NoExecute` (which evicts pods).

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` support.

### Required Implementation

Address implementation concerns in these areas:

1. **Taint Effect Constants & Enums**:
   - Find where taint effects (`NoSchedule`, `NoExecute`, etc.) are defined as constants
   - Add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` alongside them

2. **Pod Admission Logic**:
   - Find the scheduler/admission controller that checks taint effects
   - Add logic to reject pods on nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint
   - Must handle toleration matching for the new effect

3. **Endpoint Slice Update Logic**:
   - Find where service endpoints are updated based on taint effects
   - Add logic to exclude nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` from EndpointSlices
   - Ensure traffic doesn't route to tainted nodes

4. **Node Controller Logic**:
   - Verify taint effect handling in node lifecycle
   - Ensure `NoScheduleNoTraffic` doesn't trigger pod eviction (unlike `NoExecute`)

5. **Tests & Validation**:
   - Add test cases for the new taint effect
   - Verify scheduling is blocked
   - Verify traffic is redirected away from tainted nodes
   - Verify pods are NOT evicted

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand taint effect architecture**:
   - Find all definitions of taint effects constants
   - Find where `NoSchedule` and `NoExecute` are used
   - Understand the tolerance matching algorithm
   - Find endpoint slice controller logic

2. **Implement the new effect**:
   - Add `NoScheduleNoTraffic` as a new taint effect constant
   - Update all scheduler/admission checks to handle the new effect
   - Modify endpoint slice controller to exclude nodes with the new effect
   - Add Go tests covering the new behavior

3. **Verify no regressions**:
   - Existing taint effects still work correctly
   - Scheduling tests pass
   - Endpoint controller tests pass
   - Node lifecycle tests pass

## Success Criteria

[x] New taint effect `NoScheduleNoTraffic` is defined and used throughout codebase  
[x] Pods cannot be scheduled on nodes with the taint (unless they have matching toleration)  
[x] Nodes with the taint are excluded from Service EndpointSlices  
[x] Existing pods on nodes with the taint are NOT evicted  
[x] All Kubernetes tests pass  
[x] Code follows Kubernetes conventions  

## Testing

```bash
make test
```

## Comprehensive Analysis: Taint Effects in Kubernetes v1.30.0

Based on my exploration of the Kubernetes v1.30.0 codebase, here's a detailed breakdown of how taint effects are defined and used:

---

### 1. TAINT EFFECT CONSTANTS DEFINITION

**Location:** `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (lines 3510-3528)

The three taint effect constants are defined in the v1 API:

```go
// TaintEffectNoSchedule (line 3514)
TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = "NoSchedule"
// Description: Do not allow new pods to schedule onto the node unless they 
// tolerate the taint, but allow all pods submitted to Kubelet without going 
// through the scheduler to start, and allow all already-running pods to 
// continue running. Enforced by the scheduler.

// TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule (line 3518)
TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = "PreferNoSchedule"
// Description: Like TaintEffectNoSchedule, but the scheduler tries not to 
// schedule new pods onto the node, rather than prohibiting new pods from 
// scheduling onto the node entirely. Enforced by the scheduler.

// TaintEffectNoExecute (line 3527)
TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = "NoExecute"
// Description: Evict any already-running pods that do not tolerate the taint.
// Currently enforced by NodeController.
```

**Internal API:** `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (lines 3172-3185)
These are duplicated in the internal API with identical definitions.

---

**Location:** `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` (lines 3858-3878)

The validation function checks that taint effects are one of the three valid values:

## Summary: Endpoint Slice Handling of Node Taints and Traffic Routing in Kubernetes v1.30.0

Based on my exploration of the endpoint slice code in the Kubernetes v1.30.0 codebase, here's what I found:

### 1. **Endpoint Slice Building**: Where Endpoints Are Created from Pods and Nodes

**Key Files:**
- `/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler.go` (lines 170-212) - Main reconciliation loop
- `/workspace/staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/utils.go` (lines 36-72) - `podToEndpoint()` function

**Process:**
In `reconciler.go` lines 170-212, the reconciliation loop:
1. Iterates through pods matching the service selector
2. Calls `endpointsliceutil.ShouldPodBeInEndpoints(pod, true)` (line 171) to filter pods
3. Looks up the node for each pod via `r.nodeLister.Get(pod.Spec.NodeName)` (line 188)
4. Handles missing nodes - if the node doesn't exist and `PublishNotReadyAddresses` is false, the pod is skipped
5. Calls `podToEndpoint(pod, node, service, addressType)` (line 208) to create the endpoint

The `podToEndpoint()` function in `utils.go` (lines 36-72):
- Extracts pod readiness status using `endpointutil.IsPodReady(pod)` (line 38)
- Sets the endpoint's zone from node labels if available (lines 62-65)
- Sets hostname if conditions are met (lines 67-69)
- **Does NOT check node taints, node conditions, or node.Spec.Unschedulable**

### 2. **Node Ready Status Checking**

**Key Functions:**
- `isNodeReady()` in `pkg/controller/endpointslice/endpointslice_controller.go` (lines 613-621)
- `IsPodReady()` in `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/util/controller_utils.go` (lines 316-318)

**What Gets Checked:**

The node ready check exists in the controller but is **only used for topolog

Based on my thorough exploration of the codebase, I've created a detailed implementation plan at `/logs/agent/sessions/plans/nifty-puzzling-galaxy.md`. Here's the summary:

## Implementation Plan Summary

### What I Discovered

Through my exploration of Kubernetes v1.30.0, I found:

1. **Taint Effect Architecture**: Three existing effects (NoSchedule, NoExecute, PreferNoSchedule) are defined in two places:
   - `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (v1 API)
   - `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (internal API)

2. **Scheduler Enforcement**: `DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc()` currently filters for `NoSchedule` and `NoExecute` taints

3. **Critical Finding**: EndpointSlice code **does NOT currently filter nodes based on taints**. This is our main change point.

4. **Node Controller**: Uses `TaintEffectNoExecute` only for pod eviction - won't affect our new effect

### The 6-Phase Implementation Plan

**Phase 1: Add Constants** → Define `TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic` in both API types files

**Phase 2: Update Validation** → Accept the new effect in `validateTaintEffect()` function

**Phase 3: Scheduler Changes** → Include new effect in `DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc()` to block pod scheduling

**Phase 4: Endpoint Slice Logic** *(CRITICAL)* → Add node taint checking in `reconciler.go` to exclude pods from endpoints when node has the taint

**Phase 5: Verify Node Controller** → Confirm it doesn't evict pods with the new taint (no changes needed)

**Phase 6: Add Tests** → Unit and integration tests for all aspects

TAINT MATCHING LOGIC (TOLERATION CHECKING)\n\n**Location:** `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/toleration.go` (lines 29-57)\n\nCore toleration matching logic:\n\n```go\n// ToleratesTaint checks if the toleration tolerates the taint.\n// The matching follows the rules below:\n//  1. Empty toleration.effect means to match all taint effects,\n//     otherwise taint effect must equal to toleration.effect.\n//  2. If toleration.operator is 'Exists', it means to match all taint values.\n//  3. Empty toleration.key means to match all taint keys.\nfunc (t *Toleration) ToleratesTaint(taint *Taint) bool {\n    if len(t.Effect) > 0 && t.Effect != taint.Effect {\n        return false  // Effect must match if toleration specifies one\n    }\n    \n    if len(t.Key) > 0 && t.Key != taint.Key {\n        return false  // Key must match if toleration specifies one\n    }\n    \n    switch t.Operator {\n    case \"\", TolerationOpEqual:\n        return t.Value == taint.Value\n    case TolerationOpExists:\n        return true\n    default:\n        return false\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Critical Point:** Line 39-40 enforces that if a toleration specifies an effect, it MUST match the taint's effect. An empty toleration effect means it tolerates ALL effects.\n\n**Location:** `staging/src/k8s.io/component-helpers/scheduling/corev1/helpers.go` (lines 74-86)\n\nHigher-level matching function:\n\n```go\n// FindMatchingUntoleratedTaint checks if the given tolerations tolerates\n// all the filtered taints, and returns the first taint without a toleration\nfunc FindMatchingUntoleratedTaint(taints []v1.Taint, tolerations []v1.Toleration, inclusionFilter taintsFilterFunc) (v1.Taint, bool) {\n    filteredTaints := getFilteredTaints(taints, inclusionFilter)\n    for _, taint := range filteredTaints {\n        if !TolerationsTolerateTaint(tolerations, &taint) {\n            return taint, true  // Found an untolerated taint\n        }\n    }\n    return v1.Taint{}, false  // All taints are tolerated\n}\n```\n\n**Location:** `pkg/apis/core/v1/helper/helpers.go` (lines 318-341)\n\nGetMatchingTolerations function used by taint eviction:\n\n```go\n// GetMatchingTolerations returns true and list of Tolerations matching all Taints \n// if all are tolerated, or false otherwise.\nfunc GetMatchingTolerations(taints []v1.Taint, tolerations []v1.Toleration) (bool, []v1.Toleration) {\n    if len(taints) == 0 {\n        return true, []v1.Toleration{}\n    }\n    if len(tolerations) == 0 && len(taints) > 0 {\n        return false, []v1.Toleration{}\n    }\n    result := []v1.Toleration{}\n    for i := range taints {\n        tolerated := false\n        for j := range tolerations {\n            if tolerations[j].ToleratesTaint(&taints[i]) {\n                result = append(result, tolerations[j])\n                tolerated = true\n                break\n            }\n        }\n        if !tolerated {\n            return false, []v1.Toleration{}  // At least one taint is untolerated\n        }\n    }\n    return true, result\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 6. KUBELET TAINT CHECKING\n\n**Location:** `pkg/kubelet/lifecycle/predicate.go` (lines 299-302)\n\nKubelet only checks for `NoExecute` taints when admitting pods:\n\n```go\n// Check taint/toleration except for static pods\nif !types.IsStaticPod(pod) {\n    _, isUntolerated := corev1.FindMatchingUntoleratedTaint(nodeInfo.Node().Spec.Taints, pod.Spec.Tolerations, func(t *v1.Taint) bool {\n        // Kubelet is only interested in the NoExecute taint.\n        return t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute\n    })\n}\n```\n\nKubelet ignores `NoSchedule` and `PreferNoSchedule` taints - these are only enforced by the scheduler.\n\n---\n\n### 7. SUMMARY OF TAINT EFFECT USAGE\n\n| Effect | Component | Action | Behavior |\n|--------|-----------|--------|----------|\n| **NoSchedule** | Scheduler (Filter) | Hard constraint | Rejects pod scheduling on tainted node unless tolerated |\n| **PreferNoSchedule** | Scheduler (Score) | Soft constraint | Penalizes but allows scheduling; scored in scoring phase |\n| **NoExecute** | Node Lifecycle Controller + Taint Eviction Controller | Pod Eviction | Evicts running pods that don't tolerate the taint |\n\n**Key Files Summary:**\n\n1. **Definition:** `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (3510-3528), `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (3172-3185)\n2. **Validation:** `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` (3858-3878)\n3. **Scheduler Filter:** `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/tainttoleration/taint_toleration.go` (64-74)\n4. **Scheduler Score:** `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/tainttoleration/taint_toleration.go` (87-154)\n5. **Node Controller:** `pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/node_lifecycle_controller.go` (71-81)\n6. **Taint Eviction:** `pkg/controller/tainteviction/taint_eviction.go` (153-160, 469-476)\n7. **Toleration Matching:** `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/toleration.go` (29-57)\n8. **Helper Functions:** `pkg/apis/core/v1/helper/helpers.go` (318-341), `staging/src/k8s.io/component-helpers/scheduling/corev1/helpers.go` (74-86)",

:= map[endpointsliceutil.PortMapKey]endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet{}\\n169: \\n170: \\tfor _, pod := range pods {\\n171: \\t\\tif !endpointsliceutil.ShouldPodBeInEndpoints(pod, true) {\\n172: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n173: \\t\\t}\\n174: \\n175: \\t\\tendpointPorts := getEndpointPorts(logger, service, pod)\\n176: \\t\\tepHash := endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(endpointPorts)\\n177: \\t\\tif _, ok := desiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash]; !ok {\\n178: \\t\\t\\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash] = endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet{}\\n179: \\t\\t}\\n180: \\n181: \\t\\tif _, ok := desiredMetaByPortMap[epHash]; !ok {\\n182: \\t\\t\\tdesiredMetaByPortMap[epHash] = &endpointMeta{\\n183: \\t\\t\\t\\taddressType: addressType,\\n184: \\t\\t\\t\\tports:       endpointPorts,\\n185: \\t\\t\\t}\\n186: \\t\\t}\\n187: \\n188: \\t\\tnode, err := r.nodeLister.Get(pod.Spec.NodeName)\\n189: \\t\\tif err != nil {\\n190: \\t\\t\\t// we are getting the information from the local informer,\\n191: \\t\\t\\t// an error different than IsNotFound should not happen\\n192: \\t\\t\\tif !errors.IsNotFound(err) {\\n193: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn err\\n194: \\t\\t\\t}\\n195: \\t\\t\\t// If the Node specified by the Pod doesn't exist we want to requeue the Service so we\\n196: \\t\\t\\t// retry later, but also update the EndpointSlice without the problematic Pod.\\n197: \\t\\t\\t// Theoretically, the pod Garbage Collector will remove the Pod, but we want to avoid\\n198: \\t\\t\\t// situations where a reference from a Pod to a missing node can leave the EndpointSlice\\n199: \\t\\t\\t// stuck forever.\\n200: \\t\\t\\t// On the other side, if the service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses is set we just add the\\n201: \\t\\t\\t// Pod, since the user is explicitly indicating that the Pod address should be published.\\n202: \\t\\t\\tif !service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses {\\n203: \\t\\t\\t\\tlogger.Info(\\\"skipping Pod for Service, Node not found\\\", \\\"pod\\\", klog.KObj(pod), \\\"service\\\", klog.KObj(service), \\\"node\\\", klog.KRef(\\\"\\\", pod.Spec.NodeName))\\n204: \\t\\t\\t\\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\\\"skipping Pod %s for Service %s/%s: Node %s Not Found\\\", pod.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, pod.Spec.NodeName))\\n205: \\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n206: \\t\\t\\t}\\n207: \\t\\t}\\n208: \\t\\tendpoint := podToEndpoint(pod, node, service, addressType)\\n209: \\t\\tif len(endpoint.Addresses) > 0 {\\n210: \\t\\t\\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash].Insert(&endpoint)\\n211: \\t\\t}\\n212: \\t}\\n213: \\n214: \\tspMetrics := metrics.NewServicePortCache()\\n215: \\ttotalAdded := 0\\n216: \\ttotalRemoved := 0\\n217: \\n218: \\t// Determine changes necessary for each group of slices by port map.\\n219: \\tfor portMap, desiredEndpoints := range desiredEndpointsByPortMap {\\n220: \\t\\tnumEndpoints := len(desiredEndpoints)\\n221: \\t\\tpmSlicesToCreate, pmSlicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToDelete, added, removed := r.reconcileByPortMapping(\\n222: \\t\\t\\tlogger, service, existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap], desiredEndpoints, desiredMetaByPortMap[portMap])\\n223: \\n224: \\t\\ttotalAdded += added\\n225: \\t\\ttotalRemoved += removed\\n226: \\n227: \\t\\tspMetrics.Set(portMap, metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\\n228: \\t\\t\\tEndpoints: numEndpoints,\\n229: \\t\\t\\tSlices:    len(existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap]) + len(pmSlicesToCreate) - len(pmSlicesToDelete),\\n230: \\t\\t})\\n231: \\n232: \\t\\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, pmSlicesToCreate...)\\n233: \\t\\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToUpdate...)\\n234: \\t\\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, pmSlicesToDelete...)\\n235: \\t}\\n236: \\n237: \\t// If there are unique sets of ports that are no longer desired, mark\\n238: \\t// the corresponding endpoint slices for deletion.\\n239: \\tfor portMap, existingSlices := range existingSlicesByPortMap {\\n240: \\t\\tif _, ok := desiredEndpointsByPortMap[portMap]; !ok {\\n241: \\t\\t\\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlices...)\\n242: \\t\\t}\\n243: \\t}\\n244: \\n245: \\t// When no endpoint slices would usually exist, we need to add a placeholder.\\n246: \\tif len(existingSlices) == len(slicesToDelete) && len(slicesToCreate) < 1 {\\n247: \\t\\t// Check for existing placeholder slice outside of the core control flow\\n248: \\t\\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\\n249: \\t\\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\\n250: \\t\\t\\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\\n251: \\t\\t\\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\\n252: \\t\\t} else {\\n253: \\t\\t\\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\\n254: \\t\\t}\\n255: \\t\\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\\n256: \\t\\t\\tEndpoints: 0,\\n257: \\t\\t\\tSlices:    1,\\n258: \\t\\t})\\n259: \\t}\\n260: \\n261: \\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\\n262: \\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\\n263: \\n264: \\tserviceNN := types.NamespacedName{Name: service.Name, Namespace: service.Namespace}\\n265: \\tr.metricsCache.UpdateServicePortCache(serviceNN, spMetrics)\\n266: \\n267: \\t// Topology hints are assigned per address type. This means it is\\n268: \\t// theoretically possible for endpoints of one address type to be assigned\\n269: \\t// hints while another endpoints of another address type are not.\\n270: \\tsi := &topologycache.SliceInfo{\\n271: \\t\\tServiceKey:  fmt.Sprintf(\\\"%s/%s\\\", service.Namespace, service.Name),\\n272: \\t\\tAddressType: addressType,\\n273: \\t\\tToCreate:    slicesToCreate,\\n274: \\t\\tToUpdate:    slicesToUpdate,\\n275: \\t\\tUnchanged:   unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete),\\n276: \\t}\\n277: \\n278: \\tcanUseTrafficDistribution := r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations)\\n279: \\n280: \\t// Check if we need to add/remove hints based on the topology annotation.\\n281: \\t//\\n282: \\t// This if/else clause can be removed once the annotation has been deprecated.\\n283: \\t// Ref: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-network/4444-service-routing-preference\\n284: \\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\\n285: \\t\\t// Reaching this point means that we need to configure hints based on the\\n286: \\t\\t// topology annotation.\\n287: \\t\\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, events = r.topologyCache.AddHints(logger, si)\\n288: \\n289: \\t} else {\\n290: \\t\\t// Reaching this point means that we will not be configuring hints based on\\n291: \\t\\t// the topology annotation. We need to do 2 things:\\n292: \\t\\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\\n293: \\t\\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\\n294: \\t\\t//  2. Optionally remove the actual hints from the EndpointSlice if we know\\n295: \\t\\t//     that the `trafficDistribution` field is also NOT being used. In other\\n296: \\t\\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\\n297: \\t\\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\\n298: \\t\\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\\n299: \\t\\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\\n300: \\t\\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\\n301: \\t\\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\\n302: \\n303: \\t\\t// Check 1.\\n304: \\t\\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\\n305: \\t\\t\\tif r.topologyCache.HasPopulatedHints(si.ServiceKey) {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t\\tlogger.Info(\\\"TopologyAwareHints annotation has changed, removing hints\\\", \\\"serviceKey\\\", si.ServiceKey, \\\"addressType\\\", si.AddressType)\\n307: \\t\\t\\t\\tevents = append(events, &topologycache.EventBuilder{\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tEventType: corev1.EventTypeWarning,\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tReason:    \\\"TopologyAwareHintsDisabled\\\",\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tMessage:   topologycache.FormatWithAddressType(topologycache.TopologyAwareHintsDisabled, si.AddressType),\\n311: \\t\\t\\t\\t})\\n312: \\t\\t\\t}\\n313: \\t\\t\\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(si.ServiceKey, addressType)\\n314: \\t\\t}\\n315: \\n316: \\t\\t// Check 2.\\n317: \\t\\tif !canUseTrafficDistribution {\\n318: \\t\\t\\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate = topologycache.RemoveHintsFromSlices(si)\\n319: \\t\\t}\\n320: \\t}\\n321: \\n322: \\tif canUseTrafficDistribution {\\n323: \\t\\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, service.Spec.TrafficDistribution)\\n324: \\t\\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, _ = trafficdist.ReconcileHints(service.Spec.TrafficDistribution, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete))\\n325: \\t} else {\\n326: \\t\\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\\n327: \\t}\\n328: \\n329: \\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\\n330: \\tif err != nil {\\n331: \\t\\terrs = append(errs, err)\\n332: \\t}\\n333: \\tfor _, event := range events {\\n334: \\t\\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\\n335: \\t}\\n336: \\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\\n337: \\n338: }\\n339: \\n340: func NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\\n341: \\tr := &Reconciler{\\n342: \\t\\tclient:               client,\\n343: \\t\\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\\n344: \\t\\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: \\t}\\n354: \\treturn r\\n355: }\\n356: \\n357: // placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\\n358: // It only compares the specific fields we care about.\\n359: var placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\\n360: \\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\\n361: \\t\\treturn a.String() == b.String()\\n362: \\t},\\n363: \\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\\n364: \\t\\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\\n365: \\t\\t\\treturn false\\n366: \\t\\t}\\n367: \\t\\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\\n368: \\t\\t\\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\\n369: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn false\\n370: \\t\\t\\t}\\n371: \\t\\t}\\n372: \\t\\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\\n373: \\t\\t\\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\\n374: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn false\\n375: \\t\\t\\t}\\n376: \\t\\t}\\n377: \\t\\treturn true\\n378: \\t},\\n379: )\\n380: \\n381: // finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\\n382: func (r *Reconciler) finalize(\\n383: \\tservice *corev1.Service,\\n384: \\tslicesToCreate,\\n385: \\tslicesToUpdate,\\n386: \\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\\n387: \\ttriggerTime time.Time,\\n388: ) error {\\n389: \\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\\n390: \\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\\n391: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\\n392: \\t\\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\\n393: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n394: \\t\\t}\\n395: \\t\\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\\n396: \\t\\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\\n397: \\t\\t// Only update We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\\n399: \\t\\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\\n400: \\t\\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\\n401: \\t\\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\\n402: \\t\\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\\n403: \\t\\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\\n404: \\t\\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\\n405: \\t\\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\\n406: \\t\\t\\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\\n407: \\t\\t\\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\\n408: \\t\\t\\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\\n409: \\t\\t\\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\\n410: \\t\\t} else {\\n411: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n412: \\t\\t}\\n413: \\t}\\n414: \\n415: \\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\\n416: \\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\\n417: \\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\\n418: \\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\\n419: \\t\\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\\n420: \\t\\t\\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\\n421: \\t\\t\\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\\n422: \\t\\t\\tif err != nil {\\n423: \\t\\t\\t\\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\\n424: \\t\\t\\t\\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\\n425: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\treturn nil\\n426: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n427: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn fmt.Errorf(\\\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\\\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\\n428: \\t\\t\\t}\\n429: \\t\\t\\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\\n430: \\t\\t\\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\\\"create\\\").Inc()\\n431: \\t\\t}\\n432: \\t}\\n433: \\n434: \\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\\n435: \\t\\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\\n436: \\t\\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\\n437: \\t\\tif err != nil {\\n438: \\t\\t\\treturn fmt.Errorf(\\\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\\\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\\n439: \\t\\t}\\n440: \\t\\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\\n441: \\t\\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\\\"update\\\").Inc()\\n442: \\t}\\n443: \\n444: \\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\\n445: \\t\\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\\n446: \\t\\tif err != nil {\\n447: \\t\\t\\treturn fmt.Errorf(\\\"failed to delete %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\\\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\\n448: \\t\\t}\\n449: \\t\\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(endpointSlice)\\n450: \\t\\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\\\"delete\\\").Inc()\\n451: \\t}\\n452: \\n453: \\ttopologyLabel := \\\"Disabled\\\"\\n454: \\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\\n455: \\t\\ttopologyLabel = \\\"Auto\\\"\\n456: \\t}\\n457: \\tvar trafficDistribution string\\n458: \\tif r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\\n459: \\t\\tif service.Spec.TrafficDistribution != nil && *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution == corev1.ServiceTrafficDistributionPreferClose {\\n460: \\t\\t\\ttrafficDistribution = *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution\\n461: \\t\\t}\\n462: \\t}\\n463: \\n464: \\tnumSlicesChanged := len(slicesToCreate) + len(slicesToUpdate) + len(slicesToDelete)\\n465: \\tmetrics.EndpointSlicesChangedPerSync.WithLabelValues(topologyLabel, trafficDistribution).Observe(float64(numSlicesChanged))\\n466: \\n467: \\treturn nil\\n468: }\\n469: \\n470: // reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\\n471: // the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\\n472: // and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\\n473: // The logic is split up into several main steps:\\n474: //  1. Iterate through existing slices, delete endpoints that are no longer\\n475: //     desired and update matching endpoints that have changed. It also checks\\n476: //     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\\n477: //  2. Iterate through slices that have been modified in 1 and fill them up with\\n478: //     any remaining desired endpoints.\\n479: //  3. If there still desired endpoints left, try to fit them into a previously\\n480: //     unchanged slice and/or create new ones.\\n481: func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByPortMapping(\\n482: \\tlogger klog.Logger,\\n483: \\tservice *corev1.Service,\\n484: \\texistingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\\n485: \\tdesiredSet endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet,\\n486: \\tendpointMeta *endpointMeta,\\n487: ) ([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, int, int) {\\n488: \\tslicesByName := map[string]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\\n489: \\tsliceNamesUnchanged := sets.New[string]()\\n490: \\tsliceNamesToUpdate := sets.New[string]()\\n491: \\tsliceNamesToDelete := sets.New[string]()\\n492: \\tnumRemoved := 0\\n493: \\n494: \\t// 1. Iterate through existing slices to delete endpoints no longer desired\\n495: \\t//    and update endpoints that have changed\\n496: \\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\\n497: \\t\\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = existingSlice\\n498: \\t\\tnewEndpoints := []discovery.Endpoint{}\\n499: \\t\\tendpointUpdated := false\\n500: \\t\\tfor _, endpoint := range existingSlice.Endpoints {\\n501: \\t\\t\\tgot := desiredSet.Get(&endpoint)\\n502: \\t\\t\\t// If endpoint is desired add it to list of endpoints to keep.\\n503: \\t\\t\\tif got != nil {\\n504: \\t\\t\\t\\tnewEndpoints = append(newEndpoints, *got)\\n505: \\t\\t\\t\\t// If existing version of endpoint doesn't match desired version\\n506: \\t\\t\\t\\t// set endpointUpdated to ensure endpoint changes are persisted.\\n507: \\t\\t\\t\\tif !endpointsliceutil.EndpointsEqualBeyondHash(got, &endpoint) {\\n508: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tendpointUpdated = true\\n509: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n510: \\t\\t\\t\\t// once an endpoint has been placed/found in a slice, it no\\n511: \\t\\t\\t\\t// longer needs to be handled\\n512: \\t\\t\\t\\tdesiredSet.Delete(&endpoint)\\n513: \\t\\t\\t}\\n514: \\t\\t}\\n515: \\n516: \\t\\t// generate the slice labels and check if parent labels have changed\\n517: \\t\\tlabels, labelsChanged := setEndpointSliceLabels(logger, existingSlice, service, r.controllerName)\\n518: \\n519: \\t\\t// If an endpoint was updated or removed, mark for update or delete\\n520: \\t\\tif endpointUpdated || len(existingSlice.Endpoints) != len(newEndpoints) {\\n521: \\t\\t\\tif len(existingSlice.Endpoints) > len(newEndpoints) {\\n522: \\t\\t\\t\\tnumRemoved += len(existingSlice.Endpoints) - len(newEndpoints)\\n523: \\t\\t\\t}\\n524: \\t\\t\\tif len(newEndpoints) == 0 {\\n525: \\t\\t\\t\\t// if no endpoints desired in this slice, mark for deletion\\n526: \\t\\t\\t\\tsliceNamesToDelete.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\\n527: \\t\\t\\t} else {\\n528: \\t\\t\\t\\t// otherwise, copy and mark for update\\n529: \\t\\t\\t\\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\\n530: \\t\\t\\t\\tepSlice.Endpoints = newEndpoints\\n531: \\t\\t\\t\\tepSlice.Labels = labels\\n532: \\t\\t\\t\\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\\n533: \\t\\t\\t\\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\\n534: \\t\\t\\t}\\n535: \\t\\t} else if labelsChanged {\\n536: \\t\\t\\t// if labels have changed, copy and mark for update\\n537: \\t\\t\\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\\n538: \\t\\t\\tepSlice.Labels = labels\\n539: \\t\\t\\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\\n540: \\t\\t\\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\\n541: \\t\\t} else {\\n542: \\t\\t\\t// slices with no changes will be useful if there are leftover endpoints\\n543: \\t\\t\\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\\n544: \\t\\t}\\n545: \\t}\\n546: \\n547: \\tnumAdded := desiredSet.Len()\\n548: \\n549: \\t// 2. If we still have desired endpoints to add and slices marked for update,\\n550: \\t//    iterate through the slices and fill them up with the desired endpoints.\\n551: \\tif desiredSet.Len() > 0 && sliceNamesToUpdate.Len() > 0 {\\n552: \\t\\tslices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\\n553: \\t\\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\\n554: \\t\\t\\tslices = append(slices, slicesByName[sliceName])\\n555: \\t\\t}\\n556: \\t\\t// Sort endpoint slices by length so we're filling up the fullest ones\\n557: \\t\\t// first.\\n558: \\t\\tsort.Sort(endpointSliceEndpointLen(slices))\\n559: \\n560: \\t\\t// Iterate through slices and fill them up with desired endpoints.\\n561: \\t\\tfor _, slice := range slices {\\n562: \\t\\t\\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(slice.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\\n563: \\t\\t\\t\\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\\n564: \\t\\t\\t\\tslice.Endpoints = append(slice.Endpoints, *endpoint)\\n565: \\t\\t\\t}\\n566: \\t\\t}\\n567: \\t}\\n568: \\n569: \\t// 3. If there are still desired endpoints left at this point, we try to fit\\n570: \\t//    the endpoints in a single existing slice. If there are no slices with\\n571: \\t//    that capacity, we create new slices for the endpoints.\\n572: \\tslicesToCreate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\\n573: \\n574: \\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 {\\n575: \\t\\tvar sliceToFill *discovery.EndpointSlice\\n576: \\n577: \\t\\t// If the remaining amounts of endpoints is smaller than the max\\n578: \\t\\t// endpoints per slice and we have slices that haven't already been\\n579: \\t\\t// filled, try to fit them in one.\\n580: \\t\\tif desiredSet.Len() < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) && sliceNamesUnchanged.Len() > 0 {\\n581: \\t\\t\\tunchangedSlices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\\n582: \\t\\t\\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesUnchanged.UnsortedList() {\\n583: \\t\\t\\t\\tunchangedSlices = append(unchangedSlices, slicesByName[sliceName])\\n584: \\t\\t\\t}\\n585: \\t\\t\\tsliceToFill = getSliceToFill(unchangedSlices, desiredSet.Len(), int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice))\\n586: \\t\\t}\\n587: \\n588: \\t\\t// If we didn't find a sliceToFill, generate a new empty one.\\n589: \\t\\tif sliceToFill == nil {\\n590: \\t\\t\\tsliceToFill = newEndpointSlice(logger, service, endpointMeta, r.controllerName)\\n591: \\t\\t} {
  "content": "# Implementation Plan: Add NoScheduleNoTraffic Taint Effect to Kubernetes v1.30.0\n\n## Context\n\nThis task implements a new taint effect called `NoScheduleNoTraffic` that prevents pod scheduling on a node (like `NoSchedule`) AND removes the node from Service EndpointSlices (affecting traffic routing), but does NOT evict existing pods (unlike `NoExecute`).\n\nThis is distinct from:\n- **NoSchedule**: Blocks new pods but doesn't affect traffic routing\n- **NoExecute**: Blocks new pods and evicts existing ones\n- **PreferNoSchedule**: Soft constraint, doesn't block scheduling\n\nThe new effect addresses use cases where you want to gracefully drain traffic from a node without evicting pods, typically during node maintenance or lifecycle transitions.\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Add Taint Effect Constants (Definition)\n\n**Files to modify:**\n1. `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (lines 3509-3528)\n   - Add `TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic TaintEffect = \"NoScheduleNoTraffic\"` constant\n   - Add descriptive comment about the effect\n\n2. `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (lines 3162-3185)\n   - Mirror the same constant and comment in the internal API\n\n**Key detail:** The internal API in `pkg/apis/core/types.go` mirrors the v1 API and must be kept in sync.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 2: Update Taint Effect Validation\n\n**File to modify:**\n- `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` (lines 3856-3878)\n  - Function: `validateTaintEffect(effect *core.TaintEffect, allowEmpty bool, fldPath *field.Path)`\n  - Update the switch statement (line 3866) to accept `core.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic`\n  - Add the new effect to the validValues slice (lines 3869-3872)\n\n**Secondary validation checks:**\n- The toleration validation at lines 3954-3957 that restricts `TolerationSeconds` to `NoExecute` taints is correct and does NOT need modification\n- Toleration effect validation will automatically accept the new effect since it's just added to the constants\n\n---\n\n### Phase 3: Update Scheduler Pod Admission Logic\n\n**File to modify:**\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/helper/taint.go` (lines 21-28)\n  - Function: `DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc()`\n  - Update the filter to include `v1.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic` alongside `NoSchedule` and `NoExecute`\n  - This ensures the scheduler blocks pod scheduling on nodes with the new taint\n\n**Implementation:**\n```go\n// Change from:\nreturn t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule || t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute\n\n// To:\nreturn t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule || t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute ||\n       t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic\n```\n\n**Impact:** This ensures the scheduler treats `NoScheduleNoTraffic` the same as `NoSchedule` for blocking new pods.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 4: Update Endpoint Slice Filtering (Key Traffic Routing Change)\n\n**Files to modify:**\n1. `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler.go` (lines 170-212)\n   - Function: `Reconcile()`\n   - After getting the node at line 188, add a check to exclude pods on nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint\n   - Pattern: Similar to the existing check for missing nodes (lines 189-207)\n\n   **Implementation location (after line 207, before line 208):**\n   ```go\n   // Check if node has NoScheduleNoTraffic taint - if so, skip the pod\n   // to exclude it from endpoints (no traffic routing to tainted node)\n   if node != nil && hasNoScheduleNoTrafficTaint(node) {\n       if !service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses {\n           logger.Info(\"skipping Pod for Service, Node has NoScheduleNoTraffic taint\",\n               \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"service\", klog.KObj(service), \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", pod.Spec.NodeName))\n           errs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"skipping Pod %s for Service %s/%s: Node %s has NoScheduleNoTraffic taint\",\n               pod.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, pod.Spec.NodeName))\n           continue\n       }\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/utils.go` (add new helper function)\n   - Add helper function `hasNoScheduleNoTrafficTaint(node *v1.Node) bool`\n   - Implementation:\n   ```go\n   func hasNoScheduleNoTrafficTaint(node *v1.Node) bool {\n       if node == nil {\n           return false\n       }\n       for _, taint := range node.Spec.Taints {\n           if taint.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic {\n               return true\n           }\n       }\n       return false\n   }\n   ```\n\n**Critical behavior:**\n- When a node has `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint, pods on that node are excluded from EndpointSlices\n- This redirects traffic away from the node without evicting pods\n- Respects `PublishNotReadyAddresses` flag like missing nodes do (optional)\n\n---\n\n### Phase 5: Verify Node Controller Does NOT Evict\n\n**Files to check (no changes needed):**\n- `pkg/controller/tainteviction/taint_eviction.go`\n  - Function: `getNoExecuteTaints()` (lines 153-160)\n  - This function only looks for `TaintEffectNoExecute` taints\n  - `NoScheduleNoTraffic` will NOT trigger pod eviction \u2713\n\n- `pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/node_lifecycle_controller.go`\n  - All taint templates use `TaintEffectNoExecute` \u2713\n  - No changes needed\n\n---\n\n### Phase 6: Add Test Cases\n\n**New test files/functions to add:**\n\n1. **Scheduler Plugin Tests:**\n   - File: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/tainttoleration/taint_toleration_test.go`\n   - Test that pods are rejected when `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint is present\n   - Test that tolerations matching the new effect allow scheduling\n\n2. **Endpoint Slice Tests:**\n   - File: `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler_test.go`\n   - Test that pods on nodes with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint are excluded from endpoints\n   - Test that pods on nodes WITHOUT the taint are included\n   - Test interaction with `PublishNotReadyAddresses`\n\n3. **Validation Tests:**\n   - File: `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation_test.go`\n   - Test that `NoScheduleNoTraffic` is accepted as a valid taint effect\n   - Test that it can be used in tolerations\n\n4. **Integration Tests:**\n   - File: `test/integration/taint/` (if directory exists)\n   - End-to-end test showing:\n     - Pod cannot be scheduled on node with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint\n     - Pod scheduled before taint added is not evicted\n     - Traffic is redirected away from tainted node\n\n---\n\n## Critical Files Reference\n\n### Constants Definition\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (lines 3509-3528)\n- `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (lines 3162-3185)\n\n### Validation\n- `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` (lines 3856-3878)\n\n### Scheduler\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/helper/taint.go` (lines 21-28)\n- `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/tainttoleration/taint_toleration.go` (lines 64-74, 87-154)\n\n### Endpoint Slice (KEY CHANGE)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler.go` (lines 170-212)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/utils.go` (new helper function)\n\n### Node Controller (NO CHANGES)\n- `pkg/controller/tainteviction/taint_eviction.go` (verification only)\n- `pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/node_lifecycle_controller.go` (verification only)\n\n---\n\n## Verification & Testing Strategy\n\n### Unit Tests\n1. Run taint validation tests to verify new effect is accepted\n2. Run scheduler plugin tests to verify scheduling is blocked\n3. Run endpoint slice reconciler tests to verify pods are excluded from endpoints\n\n### Integration Tests\n1. Create a node with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint\n2. Verify new pod cannot be scheduled on that node\n3. Schedule a pod on the node, then add the taint\n4. Verify pod continues running (not evicted)\n5. Verify pod is removed from EndpointSlices (no traffic)\n6. Remove the taint and verify endpoint is restored\n\n### Build & Compile\n- Run: `make test` or targeted test suite for modified components\n- Compile: `go build ./staging/src/k8s.io/api/...` and `go build ./pkg/...`\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Changes by Component\n\n| Component | Change Type | Files | Key Changes |\n|-----------|-------------|-------|------------|\n| API Definition | New | 2 files | Add constant definition for NoScheduleNoTraffic |\n| Validation | Update | 1 file | Accept new effect in validation |\n| Scheduler | Update | 1 file | Include new effect in taint filter |\n| EndpointSlice | Update | 2 files | Filter nodes with new effect from endpoints |\n| Node Controller | No change | N/A | Verification only - no eviction triggered |\n| Tests | New | 3-4 files | Add test coverage for all aspects |\n\n---\n\n## Expected Behavior After Implementation\n\n### Scenario 1: Pod Scheduling\n- Pod cannot be scheduled on node with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint (unless tolerated)\n- Same behavior as `NoSchedule`\n\n### Scenario 2: Existing Pod Behavior\n- Pod running on node before taint is added: **NOT evicted** (unlike `NoExecute`)\n- Pod continues running normally\n\n### Scenario 3: Traffic Routing\n- Pod on node with `NoScheduleNoTraffic` taint: **Excluded from EndpointSlices**\n- Service traffic is redirected to other endpoints\n- Effect is visible immediately when taint is added to running node\n\n### Scenario 4: With PublishNotReadyAddresses\n- If Service sets `PublishNotReadyAddresses: true`, pods are still excluded (same as missing nodes)\n- This flag affects pod readiness, not node taint behavior\n",
  "file_path": "/logs/agent/sessions/plans/nifty-puzzling-galaxy.md"

# Implementation Plan: Add NoScheduleNoTraffic Taint Effect to Kubernetes v1.30.0

## Context

This task implements a new taint effect called `NoScheduleNoTraffic` that prevents pod scheduling on a node (like `NoSchedule`) AND removes the node from Service EndpointSlices (affecting traffic routing), but does NOT evict existing pods (unlike `NoExecute`).

This is distinct from:
- **NoSchedule**: Blocks new pods but doesn't affect traffic routing
- **NoExecute**: Blocks new pods and evicts existing ones
- **PreferNoSchedule**: Soft constraint, doesn't block scheduling

The new effect addresses use cases where you want to gracefully drain traffic from a node without evicting pods, typically during node maintenance or lifecycle transitions.

## Implementation Strategy

### Phase 1: Add Taint Effect Constants (Definition)

**Files to modify:**
1. `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (lines 3509-3528)
   - Add `TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic TaintEffect = "NoScheduleNoTraffic"` constant
   - Add descriptive comment about the effect

2. `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (lines 3162-3185)
   - Mirror the same constant and comment in the internal API

**Key detail:** The internal API in `pkg/apis/core/types.go` mirrors the v1 API and must be kept in sync.

---

### Phase 2: Update Taint Effect Validation

**File to modify:**
- `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` (lines 3856-3878)
  - Function: `validateTaintEffect(effect *core.TaintEffect, allowEmpty bool, fldPath *field.Path)`
  - Update the switch statement (line 3866) to accept `core.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic`
  - Add the new effect to the validValues slice (lines 3869-3872)

**Secondary validation checks:**
- The toleration validation at lines 3954-3957 that restricts `TolerationSeconds` to `NoExecute` taints is correc
... (truncated)
